On prosecution: **it’s uncommon** in a situation like yours, especially where **nothing was paid** and you’ve been consistent that the November bike was your friend’s and the December bike was yours. Prosecutors typically look for clear evidence of *intent to defraud* plus stronger facts than an insurance dispute.

The more likely “legal” consequences are **civil/insurance actions**, like:
- claim denial,
- policy cancellation or nonrenewal,
- being asked for documents or a recorded statement,
- or being referred to a special investigations unit for review.
